Foreign Important Telegrams

Imperial Japanese Decree Orders Suspension of Cash Redemption of Banknotes 52

If Parliament does not ratify it, it will likely be forced to dissolve; significant revisions to the previous cabinet's budget.

▲Reuter's, Tokyo, 17th - The imperial edict suspending the cash redemption of banknotes has been issued and is effective immediately. It is said that Prime Minister Inukai Tsuyoshi claims that if the Parliament does not ratify this edict, he will dissolve the Parliament and hold new elections. The cabinet today also discussed the budget. Since it is not possible to completely overhaul the next fiscal year's budget set by the previous cabinet, it has been decided to adopt its outline and make revisions. The most important revisions will be related to preserving the Ministry of Colonial Affairs and cancelling the proposed tax rate improvements.

▲United Press, Tokyo, 17th - Today, the Privy Council passed the proposal to suspend the cash redemption of banknotes, which was promulgated by Official Gazette Extra Edition Imperial Ordinance No. 291. The full text is as follows:

The Bank of Japan shall not conduct the exchange of banknotes for gold coins without the permission of the Minister of Finance. The Bank of Korea shall not conduct the exchange of Korean banknotes for gold coins without the permission of the Minister of Finance. The Bank of Taiwan shall not conduct the exchange of banknotes of the Bank of Taiwan for gold coins without the permission of the Minister of Finance. Addendum: This ordinance shall take effect from the date of promulgation.

▲Another telegram reports: Since the establishment of the Inukai Cabinet, the prices of various goods have risen across the board. The market prices of daily necessities and groceries have increased by 2.3% compared to December 1.

Dentsu News Agency, Tokyo, 17th - The Ministry of Finance held a meeting of senior officials yesterday to discuss the budget for the next fiscal year. As a result, Finance Minister Takahashi submitted the following to the cabinet today: "Revenue Department": (1) The revenue estimates remain unchanged due to time constraints. (2) The 30 million yen tax increase proposal and the 9 million yen tariff increase proposal are both suspended. (3) The revenue shortfall will be filled by issuing more government bonds and suspending the allocation to the debt reduction fund. "Expenditure Department": (1) The previous cabinet's administrative and financial reorganization will be largely followed. (2) The budget for the Ministry of Colonial Affairs will be included in this budget without fail. (3) Items that the cabinet must include in the next fiscal year's budget will be requested as supplementary budgets. (4) A 50 million yen loss from currency exchange will be included in the budget. According to this new cabinet's budget for the next fiscal year, the total amount will be more than 1.5 billion yen.

▲Dentsu News Agency, Tokyo, 17th - The group of defectors from the Seiyukai party, led by former Minister of Home Affairs Adachi, have completed the procedures for joining the Dai-ichi Kyukeishitsu (First Rest Room). As a result, the divisions of the House of Representatives are as follows: Seiyukai 251 seats, Seiyu Honto-kai 171 seats, Dai-ichi Kyukeishitsu 28 seats (including Adachi faction 10 seats, Kokumin Doshikai 6 seats, Kakushin-to 3 seats, Proletarian factions 5 seats, purely independent 4 seats, vacancies 16 seats, total 466 seats.

▲Kokumin News, Tokyo, 17th - The Tokyo Stock Exchange, which suspended trading on Monday due to the reimposition of the gold embargo, has decided to resume trading tomorrow. It is expected that the stock exchanges that have suspended trading elsewhere will resume trading tomorrow as well. The imperial ordinance to abolish the gold standard is about to be issued, and it is expected that the financial situation will stabilize somewhat within the next week. The new government has accepted the 1932 budget prepared by the previous cabinet, but with slight revisions. Parliament is scheduled to convene on December 25, and it is expected that there will be a debate on the gold embargo and the abolition of the gold standard at that time.

Suspension of Naval Shipbuilding Program 53

Under Consideration by the British Government

▲Reuter's, London, 17th - The Daily Express reported this morning that the British government is currently considering suspending the British naval shipbuilding program. Except for warships needed to counter submarines, it is proposed to suspend all construction. A small cabinet committee is currently discussing this issue. If a decision is made to suspend construction, it will be temporary and will depend on the progress of the disarmament conference in February next year. If Britain temporarily suspends shipbuilding, the British representatives attending the disarmament conference will have a strong tool to urge the reduction of European land and air forces. If the outcome of this conference is satisfactory, Britain's temporary suspension can be changed to a long-term suspension. Furthermore, if Britain's shipbuilding program is suspended, it will not only be effective at the disarmament conference but also save Britain millions of pounds. It is said that Chancellor of the Exchequer Chamberlain strongly supports this proposal. The shipbuilding program announced last March, which requires work to begin in February, includes two 7,000-ton armored cruisers, one 5,000-ton armored cruiser, one destroyer flotilla leader, eight destroyers, four troop transports, one gunboat, and two auxiliary ships.

▲Reuter's, London, 17th - The naval news reported in the Daily Express this morning has been firmly denied by the authorities and is dismissed as fantasy. The cabinet has so far only been able to touch on the fringes of the disarmament issue. Disarmament is indeed one of the issues being discussed by a small cabinet committee, but it is said that even the outline of the plan has not yet been prepared.

Misunderstanding at Burma Round Table Conference Cleared 54

▲Reuter's, London, 16th - At the Burma Round Table Conference held in London, some Burmese representatives were greatly dissatisfied when Indian Affairs Secretary Peel made remarks at a meeting last week implying that if Burma separated from India, its constitution would not be as good as the Indian constitution. This week, three representatives withdrew from the conference, expressing their determination not to participate in further discussions. In order to clear up the misunderstanding, Indian Secretary Peel stated today that the purpose of this conference is to formulate a constitution with a responsible central government. British representative Lothian also stated that the British Prime Minister's declaration on self-government at the India Round Table Conference also applies to Burma. The audience was satisfied with this statement.

Spanish Merchants Seek Loan from Britain 55

▲Reuter's, Madrid, 17th - It is reported that representatives of the Bank of England are currently in the Spanish capital discussing a British loan of 200 million pesetas. If this loan is successful, it will increase commercial relations between Britain and Spain because Spanish merchants can reduce the difficulty of finding British currency.

US Congress Begins Verbal Warfare 56

Attacking Hoover's Debt Moratorium Plan

Foreign Affairs Committee Passes Important Resolutions

▲National Press, Washington, 16th - The 72nd United States Congress began verbal warfare today. The Secretary of the Treasury, appearing before the Senate Finance Committee, stated frankly that President Hoover's government is actually opposed to the cancellation of war debts, thus sparking a heated debate with those opposing and supporting Hoover each taking their own stance. At the same time, Republican Congressman McFadden, Chairman of the House Banking and Currency Committee, criticized President Hoover, saying that Hoover and Treasury officials openly announced their opposition to the cancellation of war debts on the one hand, and secretly cooperated with debt groups on the other in an attempt to reduce the total amount of war debts. President Hoover's negotiation of a moratorium on war debt payments violated his oath of office. Republican Congressman Treadway and others strongly criticized McFadden's remarks as inappropriate. Although the moratorium on war debt payments may eventually be ratified by Congress, it has not yet been done. A total of US$122.5 million in debt owed by foreign countries to the United States is due on Tuesday. The US State Department and Treasury Department have not collected it due to prior agreements. President Hoover has now asked Congress to approve the payment of the amount owed to the United States during the moratorium period in ten years, starting on July 31, 1933.

▲National Press, Washington, 16th - The US Senate Foreign Relations Committee passed a very important foreign policy resolution today. The committee met today, chaired by Republican Senator Borah of Idaho, and unanimously passed a proposal by Republican Senator Johnson of California ordering Secretary of State Stimson to submit all State Department files regarding the Sino-Japanese Manchurian issue to the Senate for review. The US Senate Foreign Relations Committee also decided to submit it for discussion by the committee after Congress reconvenes after the Christmas and New Year holidays in preparation for public discussion by the Senate. The discussion also includes the issue of the United States joining the Hague Permanent Court. Borah announced publicly today that he would continue to work to restore diplomatic relations with Soviet Russia. It is claimed that the world economy cannot be brought into order unless the Russian problem is resolved.

Yen Hui-ching Arrives in San Francisco 57

▲National Press, San Francisco, 16th - The newly appointed Chinese Minister to the United States, Yen Hui-ching, arrived safely in San Francisco today. When he was informed that Chiang Kai-shek, Chairman of the Nanjing government, had resigned, Yen said that the new developments in China would enable China to build a stronger government. Yen spoke highly of Lin Sen, who is now acting as Chairman of the National Government. Yen also said that although the Chinese government has been reorganized, its attitude towards the Sino-Japanese issue will not change. After arriving in the United States, Yen will travel east as soon as possible in order to take office in Washington as soon as possible.

Prelude to World Islamic Unity 58

Eliminating Differences in Rituals

Actively Promoting Doctrine

▲Reuter's, Jerusalem, 17th - The World Islamic Congress, which has been meeting here for ten days, has now concluded. This meeting has made great progress in terms of Islamic unity. Representatives from all parties have eliminated minor differences in religious rituals and taken care of the larger interests of Islam, so they were able to agree on a detailed procedure. An executive committee composed of representatives from Islamic centers in various places will implement it. The Congress resolved to jointly establish an Islamic university and will engage in compiling an Arabic dictionary as the cornerstone of the Islamic revival. Rapid Advances in the Scientific World 60

Exchanging Christmas Greetings via Facsimile

▲Reuter's, London, 17th - With Christmas approaching, it is customary for friends and relatives to exchange greetings. For those in distant places, they either mail them or send them by telegram, but this is now outdated. Today, one only needs to pick up the telephone receiver, and in an instant, one can exchange greetings with relatives and friends on ships sailing the seven seas. Furthermore, one can transmit a portrait of oneself or the whole family, with handwritten greetings below, via telephone lines to friends in Austria, Denmark, Italy, Norway, and Sweden. Every 700 miles takes less than twenty minutes. The London Post Office expects the transmission of facsimiles to be very popular this year.

Romanian Prince's Romance with Commoner 61

Ultimately Obscured by Vanity, Suddenly Changes His Mind

▲Reuter's, Bucharest, 17th - The marriage of Romanian Prince Nicholas to a divorced lawyer has been reported in European newspapers for the past three weeks. According to news from here today, this matter has taken an abrupt turn. King Carol sent a letter to his younger brother Nicholas, ordering him to divorce, or else he would revoke his royal rights and all military ranks. Nicholas replied that he would rather abandon vanity and live a simple life with his lover. For a time, it was praised as a beautiful story, and many praised him for being affectionate. Unexpectedly, Nicholas has now suddenly agreed to divorce his lover. It is said that Nicholas met with his brother King Carol, and Carol agreed to restore his position as Inspector-General of the Army. As for Nicholas's sudden change of heart, it is said that it was mostly due to his mother's persuasion.

These rioters stood in front of the Party Headquarters and shouted reactionary slogans such as "Down with the Chinese Kuomintang," "Down with the National Government," and "Workers, peasants, and soldiers unite to overthrow the ruling class." Among the leaders were those who were arrested and released by Committee Members Yu and Wu on the previous day. They were carrying wooden sticks, pistols, stones, kerosene, and firewood and other weapons. After shouting for two hours, they used stones to break the Party emblem in front of the door and arrested one unarmed guard and fifteen comrades who returned to the Party Headquarters to work after lunch. The archway east of the Party Headquarters was also destroyed. As of the time of this telegram, they had not completely dispersed. Secretariat of the Central Executive Committee.

Taiyuan Student Petition Wave Subsided 64

▲Rong Honglu Acts as Mediator, Provides Satisfactory Reply

▲Normal School Experiences Expulsion of Principal Incident

Taiyuan Dispatch: All students of the Shanxi Provincial Student Anti-Japanese Federation went to the provincial government on the 11th to petition, and a conflict occurred due to a misunderstanding, destroying the doors and windows of the provincial government and belongings, as well as the residence of Miao Peicheng, the director of the education department, etc. Afterwards, the student side sent a letter to Chairman Xu that evening, expressing their apology. Yesterday (12th), all students of the Student Federation, except for those schools that had withdrawn from the event, gathered at the Provincial Confucius Temple at 9:00 AM to continue discussing the petition matters. At the same time, dozens of representatives were sent to the Army Fourth School Alumni Association to ask for a reply from Garrison Commander Rong Honglu. Rong went as scheduled and replied to the student representatives, saying, "Representatives and all students, driven by patriotic enthusiasm, are conducting a patriotic movement, which I admire very much. However, regarding the damage to the doors, windows, and belongings of the provincial government and education department yesterday, I feel ashamed and distressed because I have the responsibility to maintain law and order. I hope the representatives will tell the students that they should consider my responsibilities and also consider the country and society. As for the representatives going to Beijing to petition, I also very much agree, but the provincial government is unable to approve it due to the explicit order from the central government. If you are willing to go to Beijing, you can first submit the list of names of those going to Beijing, and I will find a way to plan travel expenses for you in a private capacity. As for the guarantee of the youth movement, the provincial government will of course agree, but within the scope that does not interfere with social order. As for the winter vacation, the Ministry of Education has regulations. If you think it is necessary to extend the vacation to conduct extensive propaganda, you should plan it yourself. Regarding the issuance of firearms, whenever you practice drills, you can borrow the number of guns used by the soldiers, and after the drills, the soldiers will take them back for their own use. As for the expenses of the Anti-Japanese Association, it is difficult for the provincial government to issue them because it involves the budget, and the students should handle it themselves in their respective schools. In short, the provincial government's committees fully support the students' patriotic enthusiasm and hope that this unfortunate incident will not happen again," and so on. The representatives felt satisfied and continued to discuss the amount of travel expenses, etc., and the maximum number of people going to Beijing to petition. After discussion, the maximum number of people should not exceed 90. Afterwards, a representative from the Normal School spoke, asking Rong to withdraw all the troops sent to the Normal School to suppress them. Rong replied that he would never interfere if the order was not disrupted. At 2:00 PM, the representatives returned to the Confucius Temple and reported the details to all the students, and prepared everything for going to Beijing. Students from various schools in the city went to the provincial government the day before to assist the petition representatives. After the students of the Normal School learned of this news, the Anti-Japanese Association of the school requested the principal to convene a general meeting to report the representatives' hunger strike. At that time, the director of student affairs of the school said that young people only need to have patriotic enthusiasm, but must not have patriotic actions, and he absolutely forbade students to gather within the scope of his duties as principal. After repeated negotiations by the student representatives, they were finally rejected. The students then gathered in the courtyard and set off in formation to the provincial government to petition and comfort the petition representatives. When they arrived at the provincial government, a representative was sent to meet them by the petition delegation, saying that the chairman was not present, and the chairman and Commander Rong had also promised a considerable reply to the matter. After the students of the school returned to school, they were very dissatisfied with Principal Liang Xianda's obstruction of the students' patriotic movement. All the students held a meeting in the courtyard, and after discussion, unanimously advocated expelling the principal from the school. Representatives from each class were elected to hold a meeting. At this time, the principal and director of student affairs had already left the school. At about 9:00 PM, troops dispatched by the Garrison Headquarters went to the school to suppress the students. Yesterday morning, the students set off from the back door, returned from the provincial government to the Confucius Temple, and requested assistance from the Student Federation. At about 1:00 PM in the afternoon, the petition delegation of the Student Federation sent a representative to report to the Confucius Temple that Commander Rong had replied that he would guarantee the return of the students of the Normal School to the school and ordered the military and police at the school not to interfere with the students' patriotic movement, but would not withdraw the troops for the time being. The students of the Normal School then obeyed the order and returned to school. (December 13)

▲More Than Two Thousand Students Gather in Yanzhou

Bengbu Declares Martial Law 66

Bengbu Dispatch: Bengbu is close to the capital, connects north and south, and is a major town in Anhui Province. Shangguan Yunxiang, the commander of the 47th Division stationed in Bengbu, recently received a telegram from Chairman Chiang ordering him to declare martial law immediately because this port is located in an important strategic location. After receiving the order, Shangguan promulgated temporary martial law regulations and implemented martial law from the 14th, and ordered the 1st Brigade under his command to dispatch two companies of troops every night to add posts and patrol back and forth in important locations, from 12:00 AM to 6:00 AM the next morning. Regardless of military or civilian personnel, no one is allowed to pass arbitrarily. Military police must have a password before they can pass. Today (15th) at 1:00 PM, Li Wenbin, the commander of the 21st Brigade of the 7th Division, Shen Yuanzhen, the director of the military police supervision office, and Zhao Chunpu, the director of the Bengbu Public Security Bureau, convened representatives of military, police, and party headquarters chambers of commerce stationed in Bengbu at a meeting at the supervision office to discuss ways to maintain law and order. (December 15)

Sudden Reorganization of the Jiangsu Provincial Government 67

▲ Summary of the New Provincial Committee

The reorganization of the Jiangsu Provincial Government this time involves significant changes. Apart from He Yushu, who continues to serve as the head of the Department of Industry, Li Mingyang is only a committee member, and it is unclear whether he will also continue to serve as the Director of the Security Bureau. The non-concurrent committee members Wang Boling and Luo Liangjian remain unchanged. Other committee members who held concurrent positions, such as Chairman Gu Zhutong, Head of the Department of Civil Affairs Zhao Qilu, Head of the Department of Finance Shu Shifu, Head of the Department of Construction Dong Xiujia, and Head of the Department of Education Cheng Tianfang, are all newly appointed. Generally speaking, many of the members of the fifth committee come from the military, which is quite different from the purely literary members of the fourth committee. Moreover, after the Executive Yuan meeting passed the decision on the 15th, a clear order was issued the next day, which is also different from the usual practice in terms of the urgency of its announcement. It is said that the new committee members are scheduled to hold an inauguration ceremony at 10:00 am on the 18th. Gu Zhutong and Ye Chucang will come to Zhenjiang today (the 17th) to handle the handover. The resumes of the new committee members are investigated as follows:

▲ Concurrently Chairman Gu Zhutong, also known as Mo San, is from Lianshui County, Jiangsu Province, and is 38 years old. He graduated from Baoding Military Academy and has served as an instructor at the Whampoa Military Academy, Commander of the 1st Division of the 1st Army of the National Revolutionary Army, Commander of the 9th Army, Member of the Military Affairs Commission of the National Government, Commander of the 2nd Division of the Army, Commander of the 2nd Army, Commander of the Guard Army, and concurrently Commander of the 1st Division.

▲ Concurrently Head of the Department of Civil Affairs Zhao Qilu, also known as Ci Hua, is from Zhenjiang. He graduated from Baoding Military Academy and has served as Chief of Staff of the 1st Army of the National Revolutionary Army, Chief of Staff of the 9th Army, and Deputy Commander of the 1st Division of the Guard Army.

▲ Concurrently Head of the Department of Finance Shu Shifu is from Cixi County, Zhejiang Province. He graduated from Baoding Military Academy and has served as an army staff adjutant, and President of the Bank of China in Fujian. He is currently a参军 in the National Government Military Council, and concurrently Director of the General Affairs Bureau. ▲ Concurrently Head of the Department of Construction Dong Xiujia, also known as Ding Yi, is from Liuhe County, Jiangsu Province, and is 39 years old. He holds a Master's degree from the University of California, USA. He has served as a professor at Shanghai China Public School, National Chengchi University, and Fudan University, English Secretary of the Shanghai-Nanjing Railway Administration, Director of the Public Works Bureau of the Wuhan Special Municipality Government, Director of the Public Utilities Bureau of the Hankou Special Municipality Government, and Counselor of the Hankou Municipal Government.

▲ Concurrently Head of the Department of Education Cheng Tianfang is from Xinjian County, Jiangxi Province, and is 32 years old. He holds a PhD in Political Science from the University of Toronto, USA. He has served as Head of the Department of Education of Jiangxi Province, Counselor of the National Government, Counselor of the Examination Yuan, Professor at National Central University, President of Anhui University, Head of the Department of Education of Anhui Province, and Deputy Minister of the Central Propaganda Department.

Educational News Special Feature

The Three Principles of the People and University Education Zheng Hongnian 81

I. General Remarks

The late Premier once said that "the foundation of revolution is built on profound learning." In other words, "revolution must have learning, and learning must also be revolutionary." The purpose of revolution is construction, and the first priority of construction is talent. The university is the cultural source and the place to cultivate talents. It should gather thousands of thoughts and create all things. It has the name of a school, and all the knowledge of the school cannot overflow the scope of the Three Principles of the People. Therefore, the Three Principles of the People are the collective crystallization of all the world's knowledge and the scale of all things. All social sciences, natural sciences, philosophy, literature, etc., related to politics, economics, and culture are subordinate to the separate and interconnected effects of the three principles of nationalism, democracy, and people's livelihood. If we want to fulfill the late Premier's legacy and earnestly promote the Three Principles of the People, then any academic field cannot do without it. May I ask, what kind of academic field is still left in the world outside the scope of the Premier's Three Principles of the People? Therefore, today's university education, known as the highest institution, only seeks to cultivate elites in the Three Principles of the People, to understand and apply them, in order to complete its mission. And today's revolutionary youth, the most promising university students in society, only seek to choose a kind of knowledge in the Three Principles of the People, to concentrate and devote themselves to it, in order to become useful talents.

II. The Spirit of the Three Principles of the People

(I) Systematizing the Old and the New The late Premier's forty years of revolutionary experience tell us to restore the inherent national spirit and self-confidence; to take the political principles of sincerity, righteousness, cultivation, family governance, and peace of the world in our country as the ultimate goal of world political philosophy; to inherit the orthodox thoughts of Yao, Shun, Yu, Tang, Wen, Wu, Duke of Zhou, and Confucius in our country, and to take the spirit of universal love as the national revolution and the human revolution, in order to realize the ideal of our nation's great unity world. The Premier founded the Republic of China and served as the leader of the revolution. With his sharp vision, he became a teacher and model for all. He inherited the traditional cultural thoughts of our predecessors and extracted the outline of the Three Principles of the People as a principle. The Western philosopher GWa　as wrote in his book "Social Heritage" that mankind sometimes uses broad and conscious efforts to measure and impart the entire inheritance of its society, and to make the new and the old become a systematic relationship, such as Greece in the time of Socrates, Italy in the Renaissance, and France in the revolutionary era. Therefore, revolution is not difficult. It is difficult to revolutionize and to make the new and the old become a systematic relationship, to measure and impart the entire inheritance of its society. The French Revolution destroyed for more than eighty years, and Mr. Wah still enjoyed praising it. If he was born today and understood the true meaning of the late Premier's revolution, then he would not know how to praise it. Alas, the Premier's doctrine is broad and profound, inheriting the past and opening up the future. It is rooted in the old cultural thoughts of our country for thousands of years and develops the new era trend of the 20th century. From its horizontal perspective, it is the survival of the fittest; from its vertical perspective, it is eternal survival.

(II) Striving, Not Struggling The Premier devoted his life to revolution, and even on his deathbed, he had to call out, "Peaceful struggle to save China." To save China, we must struggle, and struggle must be carried out peacefully. If struggle cannot be peaceful, it will evolve into strife, which will violate the late Premier's legacy of universal love. The Book of Rites says, "Strive to the light of supreme virtue." The Book of Changes says, "A thunder comes out of the ground, stirring." This striving has the meaning of promoting and shocking. Its way is supreme and firm. The Analects says, "What a gentleman strives for." This striving is not the same as struggling. I still remember that,

"King Xiang said to King Han, "The world has been in turmoil for several years because of us two. I am willing to challenge King Han to determine the outcome, rather than making the people of the world suffer for nothing." King Han smiled and said, "I would rather fight wits than fight strength." (See Historical Records)

Fighting wits is striving, and fighting strength is struggling. Striving has the spirit of intelligence, advancement, benevolence, courage, and perseverance. Struggling is an act of cruelty, brutality, violence, and plunder. The division between striving and struggling can be thought of more than half way here.

(III) Saving the World with Peace The Premier's goal of national revolution is not only to seek the liberation of all ethnic groups in the country, but also to seek the freedom and equality of all mankind in the world, so as to ascend to the great unity. Looking at the international situation, it is getting worse and worse. The United Kingdom and Germany are now in deep water. Their suffering from foreign economic oppression is almost the same as our suffering from the military force of the Japanese Empire. During the world economic crisis, which has evolved into an international political problem, the social system is tending towards stagnation. The current organization is approaching its end. The future is worrisome and peace is difficult to achieve. Only the Three Principles of the People is the ladder of peaceful evolution and the savior in desperation. Taking the land problem as an example, scholars around the world have exhausted their brains, but it is still difficult to solve. China implemented the well-field system in the Zhou Dynasty, the king's field system in the Han Dynasty, the equal-field system in the Northern Wei Dynasty, and the official-field system in the Southern Song Dynasty. However, although there were many systems, the implementation was ineffective, causing only trouble. In the end, it still flowed into a bad private system. The Premier, based on the principle of equality, used peaceful methods to implement equal land rights, creating a new system unprecedented in thousands of years. In addition, he restrained capital, eliminated monopolies, developed public services, enriched the country and the people, solved China's social problems, and gave the world the same goal. That is, to advance and cooperate with all mankind in the world, to seek the fair distribution of wealth, so that they can live and work in peace and realize the world of the people, ruled by the people, and enjoyed by the people. Therefore, we who follow the late Premier's legacy must not forget the late Premier's entire purpose of national revolution, which is to save the world, so that the late Premier's spirit of saving the world with peace will not be obscured by distortion and misunderstanding, and can be fully revealed to the world, to gain international sympathy, and at least to avoid the rampant extreme thoughts of communism and nationalism in the country, and to avoid the cyclical aggression of imperialism abroad. If the imperialists can understand the implementation of the Three Principles of the People in our country, the pursuit of national salvation, and the pursuit of the people's Three Principles of the People and University Education (to be continued)

A Contradictory Phenomenon in the Cry for National Salvation - Hai Chang 82

▲ Teachers, Students, and Various Provinces

National salvation cannot be achieved through empty talk, nor through pasting slogans, shouting slogans, boycotts, parades, telegrams, or declarations. All those engaged in national salvation work must have a genuine expression of patriotism, setting an example with unwavering commitment. Only then will their words and actions be credible and effective. Otherwise, even before five minutes have passed, no one will believe they are truly saving the country.

Currently, the most enthusiastic and sacrificing group in the cause of national salvation is undoubtedly the students. The students' patriotic fervor is, of course, the result of education. It is already a pitiful state when only a few intellectuals are enthusiastic about saving the country, running around and calling for action, when the nation is in such danger. But can these few saviors of the country be trusted for their genuine expression of patriotism? I dare not answer. Look at the current college students; almost none of them are without Western suits and leather shoes. Almost none of the female students are without foreign coats and high-heeled leather shoes. Almost all the materials adorning them are foreign goods. The patriotic youth claim to be overthrowing imperialism every day, yet they are also very eager and respectful in offering money to imperialists, buying and wearing their decorative materials, considering themselves fashionable and glorious. What a self-contradictory act of national salvation!

Because the youth saviors of the country have such self-contradictory behaviors, their sacrifices cannot be forgiven by the government or trusted by the people. The government's disapproval has become obvious recently, and the people's lack of sympathy may be doubted. However, students who have been to the countryside to promote the cause should know how cold the villagers are towards us. And we must know that these villagers still account for more than 80% of the national population. Once, when students were giving a speech in the countryside about boycotting Japanese goods, the villagers said, "We villagers have never used foreign goods. It would be good if you students yourselves don't use Japanese goods." Indeed, let's now compare a male or female student who talks about patriotism all the time with an ignorant country bumpkin or village girl who doesn't know what patriotism is. One is wearing a foreign hat, suit, watch, fountain pen, leather shoes, coat, etc., with nothing on their body that isn't a foreign product. The other is wearing a cloth hat, blue cloth shirt and pants, cloth shoes, etc., unable to find a single foreign product on their body. Comparing the two, who is patriotic and who is not?

There have already been eight or nine boycotts of Japanese goods. The longest boycott lasted no more than six months, and before and after the boycott, imports of Japanese goods routinely surged, so the effect was ultimately equal to zero. The reason for the ineffectiveness of these boycotts is clearly that the Chinese people do not have the determination to use domestic goods, especially the young men and women who claim to be patriotic. Their words and actions do not match, and their worship of foreign goods is too strong. So today, they are bullied by the Japanese and boycott Japanese goods, using British or other foreign goods. Tomorrow, they are bullied by the British and boycott British goods, using Japanese or other foreign goods. Boycotting back and forth only enriches foreigners. China's economic leakages are only increasing year by year, and the phenomenon of poverty is only intensifying year by year. Even without the military aggression of imperialism, the bankruptcy of China's national economy is already apparent.

China's science is underdeveloped, and the import of foreign machinery and various industrial products is a natural trend. Only clothing materials are readily available in China, so there is really no need to use foreign goods. Ever since the psychology of wearing Western suits as fashionable was actively promoted by the education sector, it has become very common among all classes in the country. Wearing Western suits and using foreign materials is, of course, not surprising. But wearing Chinese clothing and using broadcloth to make mandarin jackets and serge to make robes, or georgette and Indian silk to make cheongsams, is really unnecessary. Since foreign goods have already "clothed China," the original silk industry has plummeted, and the sales of native cloth have almost been cut off. If there were no foreign clothing materials imported now, a large part of China would have to be naked.

The trend of Chinese people wearing Western suits has only been popular for the past twenty years. Forty years ago, first-class Chinese diplomats such as Li Hongzhang and Zeng Jize, and first-class students studying abroad such as Yan Fu and Gu Hongming, still wore Chinese clothing and dragged their braids when they were abroad. Twenty years ago, although students studying abroad wore Western suits, they changed back to Chinese clothing after returning to China. The braids were cut off and could not be reattached, so a fake little braid was put in a small hat. People today may say they were stubborn, but they were indeed knowledgeable in both Chinese and Western learning. Their attitude of "a gentleman studies extensively and dresses according to his homeland" is beyond the reach of ordinary students studying abroad today. Since the President So-and-so and Empress So-and-so ships brought back hundreds and thousands of gilded PhDs and masters one after another, people would not know how "broad" and how "masterful" they were except for their foreign language and writing. So they absolutely refuse to wear Chinese clothing, showing that they are extraordinary and superior. The greatest use of these PhDs and masters, of course, is to teach in schools, so college students, middle school students, and even elementary school students all follow the example of their teachers' attire, preparing to become future PhDs and masters. So foreign firm clerks, company runners, and even hooligans, gigolos, and prostitutes also dress in Western suits and leather shoes, pretending to be new figures of the new era. Since Western suits have stolen the show, the outdated Chinese clothing is only worn by country bumpkins, village women, and people who have no money. Fortunately, the number of students is still a very small minority of the national population. When education becomes truly universal in the future, it will be the day when Chinese clothing is completely eliminated. At that time, all domestic silk shops and native cloth shops will have to close, and the workers who make domestic clothing materials will starve to death. (To be continued)

Zhejiang Provincial Government Safeguards Education Funds 83

▲ Salary Reduction for Teachers and Staff Not Yet Considered

▲ Order Already Issued to the Finance Department for Compliance

The Zhejiang Provincial Government, due to a budget shortfall of six to seven million for this year, proposed to reduce the expenses of all agencies to 75% as a standard remedy. This led to petitions from teachers and staff of Hangzhou County Normal School, Provincial High School, and First Middle School, arguing that reducing education funding would hinder education. They presented eight points of difficulty to the Provincial Government, requesting exemption from the reduction. The Provincial Government believes that education is related to the foundation of the country and should be vigorously safeguarded. As for reducing the salaries of teachers and staff, it has not yet been considered. An instruction was issued to the teachers and staff of the said schools and to the Finance Department for compliance. The original order is transcribed as follows: According to the petitions submitted by Wang Yiwen, Yuan Yi, and other teachers and staff of the Provincial High School and Hangzhou Normal School, requesting that the education funds be exempted from reduction and that monthly payments be made to maintain and benefit education, etc., in response to this, it is hereby notified that the province's finances are extremely difficult, and the amount of the shortfall between income and expenditure this year has reached six to seven million. It is necessary to reduce all budget items as much as possible to maintain. As education is related to the foundation of the country, the government will spare no effort to safeguard all education funds in the province within the possible scope. The salary reduction for staff has not yet been considered. In addition to ordering the Finance Department to issue the education funds on a monthly basis, it is hereby notified, etc. After the instruction is posted, the original petition is copied and sent to the said department for compliance. This order.

Local News

Shanghai Education Community's Joint National Salvation Association's Letter of Advice to Students to Resume Classes 84

The Shanghai Education Community's Joint National Salvation Association's Letter of Advice to Students to Resume Classes states: Since the National Government established its capital in Nanjing in the sixteenth year of the Republic of China, it was thought that China would eliminate all malpractices, alleviate the people's distress, recuperate and nurture the national foundation, unite our nation, promote our civil rights, and work together to solve the people's livelihood problems in order to reach a state of great harmony. The people's desire for governance was so great that the clouds and rain in a great drought were not enough to describe even one hundredth of it. Who would have thought that the political program would be lost, and villains would fill the court? Reciting Mencius's words, "When the ruler has no moral standards, the subjects have no laws to follow. The court does not believe in the Way, and the craftsmen do not believe in the rules. Gentlemen commit offenses against righteousness, and commoners commit crimes against the law," how can one not be heartbroken? We have often sighed while teaching. Our young students, seeing that China has the pain of sinking and fearing that the overturned nest will have no intact eggs, throw down their pens and books, and rise up resolutely, spending the light of an inch of jade and making desperate calls with bare hands. Petitioning, propaganda, and fundraising, braving frost and dew and eating and sleeping in the wind without taking care of themselves. This spirit of pure sacrifice, righteousness, courage, and patriotism is sympathized with by all Chinese people, especially we who have close ties with you and know each other well. However, the current situation is gradually developing. Issues such as the neutralization of Jinzhou, joint management of Tianjin, and direct negotiations may not be realized for the time being, and Chiang Kai-shek also knows that the country's affairs are difficult and the future is hard, so he retreats bravely and telegraphs his resignation. Our young students, at this juncture, should resolutely jump out of the whirlpool, cleanse their bodies, restrain their thoughts, and cultivate their morals, so as to become great talents. Who else but you can shoulder great responsibilities? The most urgent task of the current government is to organize everything in an orderly manner, so that it can be transformed. Only by concentrating the spirit can it be organized. The tranquility of the people can concentrate the spirit. The responsibility of awakening the people and urging the government is fulfilled. In the future, the government should be responsible for renewing national politics and broadly planning the national economy, and give it sufficient time. In addition to chanting, we should still adhere to our supervisory responsibilities. Studying without forgetting national salvation has already been done by you. Saving the country without forgetting to study is what we hope you will continue to do. The ancients said that wealth and honor cannot corrupt, poverty and meanness cannot move, and power and force cannot subdue. It also said that one anger makes the princes fear, and peaceful residence makes the world calm. It also said to be as still as a virgin and as fast as a fleeing rabbit, to advance with righteousness and retreat with propriety, to be able to release and able to收. This is the business of a great man, the conduct of a great man. Let's further verify it with historical facts. Advancing is like a tide, and retreating is like a mountain. This is why Yue Fei's army was able to establish extraordinary achievements. Zhang Mai rose up in anger, but was outwardly strong and inwardly weak, unable to advance or retreat, unable to maneuver. This is why the Jin army was defeated miserably. You, you, think it over carefully. In short, in our humble opinion, the government's past mistakes do not need to be concealed. The spirit of your patriotism cannot be criticized. But today, you should rein in your horses and turn movement into stillness, giving the current government time to work and advancing your own morals. This is the only way forward. I especially offer my sincere advice and hope that you will think deeply and carefully with a calm mind. How fortunate, how fortunate!

Another Statement from Aurora University 87

Aurora University sent a letter yesterday stating: Dear Editor, after reading the education news column in today's newspaper, the letter from the Aurora Anti-Japanese Association contained statements that were completely untrue. The school has never adopted any repressive measures against students' anti-Japanese work. When the Anti-Japanese Association was established, it even donated a large sum of money. Students were allowed to hold meetings, discuss, post notices, and conduct propaganda freely without any obstruction. Military training has also been specially intensified, increasing to six hours per week. As for those who stayed in school after the holiday, there are still 78 non-religious students and only 31 religious students. The lists are available for verification. The statements in the letter are nothing more than fabrications from one or two irresponsible students who intend to confuse the public. If there are any more such inaccurate records in the future, we will ignore them to avoid the labor of correction. Sincerely, Aurora University, December 17th.

The Chinese Race Walking Association Initiates Women's Race Walking 89

▲ Length of 3,200 Meters, Registration Starts on January 10th, Race on February 21st

丨Simultaneously with a 13-Mile Long Run丨

This year, the Chinese team won the championship and individual first place in the International Race Walking Competition, and set a new record of two hours, twenty-seven minutes, and three seconds. The championship has been won for four consecutive years, which is an unprecedented honor. Moreover, the entire Chinese team finished the race without anyone dropping out halfway, which is truly commendable. The Chinese Race Walking Association, in view of the interest in race walking and its value in international sports, and to promote it, has specially initiated an open 13-mile long-distance race walking competition in Shanghai, scheduled to be held on Sunday, February 21st next year. The route is exactly the same as the International Race Walking Competition, but it turns back from Huaihai Road and ends at the Chinese Athletics Field on Route Tenant de la Tour. (Detailed route map will be published later) At the same time, a women's open race walking competition will be held, the length of which is 3,200 meters, or about two miles, which is also to promote women's sports. Registration will start on January 10th. Non-members who join must pay 20 cents at the time of registration, and women's race walking is free. As for women's race walking, because it is an initiative, it is expected that there will be no shortage of participants from the many women's physical education schools in Shanghai. However, if there are concerns that the posture is not very clear, the association will send experienced personnel to provide voluntary guidance for schools and groups that send letters.

Sun Ke and His Entourage Went to Beijing Yesterday Morning 93

▲ Sun Ke Arrived in Beijing to Issue a Joint Statement

▲ The Committees Remaining in Guangdong Are Expected to Arrive in Shanghai Around the 20th

Guangdong representatives Sun Zhesheng, Wu Tiyun, Zou Haibin, Chen Youren, Li Junpei, and five other representatives, after Chiang's resignation, at the invitation of central representatives He Yaozu and others, took a special train prepared for the Jinghu Railway with Chen Gongbo, Gu Mengyu, and other twenty central committee members at 9:30 yesterday morning, and arrived in Beijing at 3:40 yesterday afternoon, and will prepare for the first plenary meeting of the Fourth Central Committee in Beijing on the 21st of this month. The situation yesterday is recorded below.

▲ The Railway Bureau Prepares the Train　The Jinghu and Huhangyong Railway Administrations, at the request of Mr. He Yaozu the other day, prepared the train to welcome the Guangdong representatives to Beijing. Immediately, a flower car was prepared, consisting of one PCMI flower car, one PCm2 flower car, one FD545 first-class car, one FD546 first-class car, one FCP584 first-class car, and one third-class car and one dining car, a total of eight cars, all of which were prepared the other night.

From right to left, front row: Wu Chaochu, Sun Ke, Zou Lu, Li Wenfan, Zeng Zhongming, Gan Naiguang, Tang Shengzhi, Chen Gongbo, Xu Minyi. Back row: Fu Bingchang, Chen Youren

Besides Principal He Shizhen, many representatives from the Fourth and Ninth District Volunteer Corps, various labor unions, and academic circles in this city were present. ▲Sun and Chen Arrive at the Station 95

The trains were originally scheduled to depart at 9:00 AM yesterday. Others boarded one after another. Also traveling with them were Wang Faquan, Pan Yunchao, Bai Ti, Ji Zhuqing, Gan Naiguang, Chuan Rulin, Guo Chuntao, Mao Zuquan, Gan Jiehou, Wen Jiangang, and over two hundred attendants. Zhao Pilian, Chen Jiayou, Li Liejun, Cheng Qian, Qin Zhen, Ju Zheng, and Fang Zhenwu were all scheduled to go to Beijing on the 20th. Liu Luyin had not yet set a date. Xie Chi was recuperating in Hangzhou.

▲The Scene at the Platform 96

When the representatives boarded the special train at the third platform, it was guarded by tax police from the temporary Zhabei police station. The special train originally had only seven cars. At 8:40 AM, due to the large number of passengers going to Beijing, Chen Bijun, Chu Minyi, Wang Faqin, Zeng Zhongming, Chen Gongbo, and Gu Mengyu shared car PCm1, while Sun Ke, Wu Chaochu, Zou Lu, Li Wenfan, Chen Youren, Fu Bingchang, Chen Jianru, Zhong Tianxin, He Yaozu, and others shared flower car PCM2. An armored train had already departed five minutes earlier to clear the tracks. The Railway Bureau specially assigned Xu Shibin to accompany and entertain the passengers. It was reported that yesterday's lunch, one hundred and twenty Western-style meals, was pre-ordered by the Guangdong Liaison Office in Shanghai to feed those who had registered the day before yesterday. Photography reporters from various Shanghai newspapers also went to Beijing, so the total number of people was about three hundred or more.

▲Zou Lu's Remarks 97

When Zou Lu arrived at the station and saw the Volunteer Corps standing tall and spirited to see them off, Zou Lu gave them words of encouragement and expressed his apologies before hurrying onto the train. The reporter met Zou on the train and conducted an interview. According to Zou, about ninety people were traveling together today. Mr. Wang (Jingwei) would probably not be able to depart in the next two or three days. His condition was the same as before, but slightly better. Mr. Xie Huiseng is currently recuperating in Hangzhou and is expected to send news soon and will also go to Beijing. The First Plenary Session of the Central Executive Committee is scheduled to open on the 21st. After the meeting, I may need to come to Shanghai again. Mr. Hu Zhantang has not yet announced his departure date from Hong Kong. Shanghai has now appointed adjutants Feng Ciqi and Liang Qingyun to be responsible for entertaining the Central Committee members coming from Guangdong.

▲Chen Gongbo's Remarks 98

According to Chen Gongbo's conversation with the reporter from the New Voice Society in the train, he had spent most of his time overseas in Belgium. After returning to China, he had only been back for two months. He arrived in Shanghai from Hong Kong on the 7th of this month. The fact that the Central Committee members going to Beijing could gather together was a blessing for the future of the country. As for Mr. Wang (Jingwei)'s condition, doctors have examined him and found that his urine contains about 197 parts of sugar, while normal people only have about 70 parts. If it increases by another ten parts or so, it could lead to a coma. Doctors have instructed him to rest and recuperate for the time being, so Mr. Wang will not be able to go to Beijing for the time being.

▲Welcome in the Capital 99

After arriving in the capital, those who welcomed them at the station included Lin Sen, Shao Lizi, Yu Youren, and Lian Shenghai. They immediately went to the Ministry of Railways. After arriving at the Ministry of Railways, a discussion meeting was immediately held.

▲Joint Statement 100

After Sun, Wu, and others arrived in Beijing, they issued a joint statement saying, "Our only task in coming to Beijing this time is to prepare for the convocation of the Fourth Plenary Session of the Central Executive Committee to implement the various resolutions of the Shanghai Peace Conference. The Fourth Plenary Session of the Central Executive Committee is a major turning point for our country to discard the old and embrace the new. If it can be realized, the resolutions of the Shanghai Peace Conference will open up a new path for future politics. You are all very clear about this point. As for the current diplomatic problems, we have repeatedly declared that we will strive to achieve the goal of restoring territorial sovereignty with the spirit of not losing our rights or humiliating the country, and with perseverance and unwavering determination, in order to live up to the expectations of the people. This is our duty. This time when we come to Beijing, we will have a clearer understanding of the dangers of the Northeast Three Provinces incident. After the establishment of a unified government, we believe that we will be able to respect public opinion, and with the people united, we will be able to exert the spirit of revolutionary diplomacy and employ the military strategies of revolutionary diplomacy to restore the territorial sovereignty of the Northeast Three Provinces. If necessary, we believe that the new government will make the greatest determination and will never fail to live up to the expectations of the people. As for the loss of the Northeast Three Provinces this time, the military and political authorities directly responsible for defending the territory should bear the responsibility and be judged by the public."

Anti-Japanese National Salvation News Yesterday 117

The city's Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association convened its 29th Standing Committee meeting at 2:00 PM yesterday. The resolutions of the meeting are as follows: (1) Song Shaoji submitted a case that the association's inspectors Yang Haichang, Wu Ziping, and Xiao Tingyun extorted bribes from Xiangtaihao and submitted evidence for investigation. How should this case be handled? It was resolved that there was evidence that the two inspectors, Wu Ziping and Xiao Tingyun, accepted bribes, and they should be dismissed immediately, and photos should be taken to show the public and announce their crimes. The two inspectors investigated Yang Haichang and inspectors of the industry association to see if they were suspected of accepting bribes. However, the two committee members, Lu Jingshi and Li Yongxiang, should reinvestigate. (2) The Cotton Cloth Industry Association sent a letter stating that, according to letters from fellow businesses, the products of Lun Chang Company were sealed by fellow businesses. Recently, the association's announcement stated that the materials were Japanese goods and that the property rights belonged to British merchants, which was ambiguous. Can the company's products be unsealed and sold? Also, the goods sealed by fellow businesses, although they are Japanese goods, the property rights already belong to Chinese merchants, so they can of course be unsealed and sold. The situation is reported and it is hoped that a reply will be provided. How should this case be handled? It was resolved to submit it to the Executive Committee. (3) A letter from Mink Company asked to forward a letter to anti-Japanese associations in various places to prove whether the company's products should be approved. It was resolved to decide that if there are facts, it can be certified on behalf of the company. (4) The Investigation Department was tasked with investigating whether the Yunzhou Factory had registered with the association. It was immediately investigated that the factory's books and registration form matched the association's registration form, so the yarn was indeed registered correctly. It was resolved to return the sealed documents after the matter was presented to the meeting for verification. (5) A letter from the Yarn Industry Association asked whether the Japanese yarn that was imported before the Anti-Japanese Association was established should be allowed to be sold publicly by the association. It was resolved to resolve this issue together after the regulations for sealing Japanese goods are formulated. (6) A letter from Ruifenghao asked to return the detained non-Japanese goods as soon as possible. It was resolved to investigate the case and release the goods.

Lawyers' Association Holds Joint Executive and Supervisory Committee Meeting for National Crisis 118

The Shanghai Lawyers' Association, in response to the recent tense situation and to deal with the national crisis, convened its 95th temporary emergency joint meeting of executive and supervisory committee members at 9:00 PM last night. Lu Shaozong presided over the meeting, and Dai Jiguang recorded it. After the chairman reported the purpose of the meeting, Li Shirui, a committee member, reported on his participation in the national crisis meetings in various provinces and expressed his opinions on dealing with the national crisis and saving the country. The committee members present were asked to carefully study and discuss the results, hoping that the authorities would propose specific policy guidelines to show the people of the country. The important points are recorded below: (1) How to permanently end the civil war and stabilize people's livelihood; (2) How to implement constitutional government and promote civil rights; (3) How to recover lost territory and complete the country; (4) How to determine foreign policy and enhance international status; (5) How to strengthen national defense and reform the military system; (6) How to reorganize finances and publicize audits; (7) How to eliminate class struggle; (8) How to popularize education and inspire national talent; (9) How to revitalize industry and develop production; (10) How to reorganize the judiciary and protect human rights; (11) How to relieve disaster victims and prevent disasters; (12) How to develop transportation to facilitate transportation; (13) How to strengthen the border areas and prevent coveting; (14) How to rejuvenate internal affairs and rectify officialdom. The above fourteen cases were resolved and passed, and Committee Member Li Shirui was immediately appointed to draft a declaration and public announcement to the people of the country, and to submit a draft to the National Government requesting prompt policy guidelines to the Standing Committee for review and issuance. The meeting adjourned late at night.

▲Overseas Chinese in Iloilo Telegraph 5,000 Taels 120

Collection of Winter Grain Tax Begins in City and County 143

The Shanghai winter grain tax collection office began operations on the 16th. However, the office found that the amount of old arrears was considerable. Yesterday, it instructed all tax collection police officers to urge taxpayers to pay off their debts as soon as possible. Furthermore, the office stated that in the past, taxpayers in the city would present their grain receipts to the office for payment. Now, some land deeds from various "bao tu" (neighborhood units) have been found to be altered or replaced. Therefore, a special notice is issued to all those who have obtained certificates, stating that when paying the grain tax for the first time, they should bring their certificates to the office for verification. If the original certificates are pledged elsewhere, they should declare the name of the household and the number of mu (unit of land area) to the office for comparison with the new receipts. After verification, the grain tax can be paid, and the receipts will be issued.

Furthermore, the Shanghai County Finance Bureau issued a notice yesterday, stating: "According to the autumn harvest records this year, the provincial committee went to various villages to conduct a survey, together with the bureau, and requested that the grain tax of the entire county be reduced by 0.7%. The Finance Department has approved this request, and it has been announced. Now, the winter grain tax collection for the 20th year of the Republic has been announced on the 5th of this month. Therefore, the reduction in tax rate based on the autumn survey is announced for the information of all grain households in the county."

Impersonating Detectives to Extort Two Thousand Dollars 145

▲ Zhang Jifu led a group armed with guns

▲ Wu Zhuohui was terrified

▲ First borrowed a hundred foreign dollars to hand over

▲ Then reported to the police, who made arrests

Wu Zhuohui, a 28-year-old native of Jinhua, Zhejiang, and former head of the Zhejiang Anti-Smuggling Brigade, resides on the third floor of No. 1 Lianyi Fang, Avenue Joffre, French Concession. On the morning of the 12th of this month, at 9:00 AM, Zhang Jifu, a native of Shaoxing, residing at No. 234 Gonghe Road, Zhabei, and Tong Jianzhong, a native of Taizhou, residing at No. 1 Ruihua Fang, Rue Bayle, French Concession, and Qiu Yaoshan, a native of Shaoxing, along with five others, carrying handguns, impersonated detectives from the French Police and the Garrison Headquarters. They went to Wu's house and claimed that the National Government had offered a reward of 5,000 yuan for his arrest because he had impersonated a division commander. They said that if he paid 2,000 yuan, they could settle the matter privately and report that he had moved out. Wu was terrified and, having no money at home, borrowed 100 foreign dollars from a friend and handed it over. They agreed to pay the remaining amount at 1:00 PM on the 15th. On the morning of the 16th, at 9:00 AM, Zhang and his gang went to collect the money again. Wu notified the doorman, Shi Baorong, who reported to the police. The police dispatched detectives and arrested Zhang and his two accomplices. The police found Jiangsu Security Team badges, letters of appointment, photographs, and other items on the three men. Yesterday morning, they were sent to the First Court of the Second Special District, where Judge Luo Renji interrogated them. Gu Shouxi, the police lawyer, stated the case, saying that the defendants had impersonated police detectives to extort money from the plaintiff by intimidation. He requested that they be prosecuted under Articles 165 and 370 of the Criminal Law. However, two other accomplices had not been apprehended, and the handguns had not been recovered. He requested that the hearing be postponed. The plaintiff, Wu Zhuohui, testified that when the defendants came, there were six of them. They showed him Jiangsu Security Team cards. When they saw that he had two handguns, the first defendant claimed to be a special detective from the police, and the third defendant said he was a detective from the Garrison Headquarters. They said he had impersonated the Seventh Division Commander of Guangdong, and the National Government had issued a warrant for his arrest with a reward of 5,000 yuan. They had orders to arrest him with the police. The second defendant pulled him into the room and said, "Are you willing to pay 2,000 yuan to settle the matter privately?" They sent accomplices to guard the door and the stairs to prevent family members from entering or leaving. He was intimidated and had no choice but to agree. Because he had no money at home, he invited his friend Hu Shuanglai from the Oriental Hotel to borrow 100 foreign dollars, which he gave to the second defendant. He agreed to pay the remaining 1,900 yuan at 1:00 PM on the 15th and was told to move and hide temporarily. They left at 3:00 PM. On the morning of the 16th, at 9:00 AM, the defendants came to collect the money again. He had notified the doorman in advance, who reported to the police, and they were arrested. The witness, Shi Baorong, testified that on the 15th, he saw the defendants go to Wu's place and then saw Wu sending them off, looking worried. The second defendant held his hand. After they left, he asked Wu what had happened. Wu told him to be on guard and report to the police if they came again. The defendants came again on the 16th, and he reported to the police and they were arrested. Under interrogation, the defendant Zhang Jifu confessed that he was a military detective in the Jiangsu Security Team and was currently on leave. Tong confessed that he had worked in the military and was now unemployed. Qiu confessed that he was formerly the director of the Meixi Public Security Bureau. All denied impersonating and extorting money. The interrogation was adjourned. Judge Luo ordered the defendants to be detained and scheduled a new hearing.

▲ Effective January Next Year

The city-operated Pujiang Ferry from Shanghai to Donggou has ticket prices largely based on the old Pujiang Embankment Works Relief. Therefore, they submitted a report to the municipal government, which approved a reasonable increase or decrease in ticket prices at each pier based on distance. The prices from Shanghai to Donggou will be changed to 12 cents for second class, 25 cents for first class, and 40 cents for special class. Shanghai to Xidu and Xidu to Donggou will be 7 cents for second class, 12 cents for first class, and 30 cents for special class. Xidu to Gaoqiao will be 10 cents for second class, 22 cents for first class, and 40 cents for special class. These measures will take effect on January 1 of next year.

Methods for Preventing and Treating Coal Poisoning 148

▲ Notice from the Municipal Health Bureau

The Municipal Health Bureau, in view of recent reports of residents in the city dying from coal poisoning, has issued a notice in vernacular Chinese, stating: "In the cold winter, many households have stoves in their homes. If one is not careful, they can be poisoned by coal gas, endangering their lives, which is very frightening. Our bureau wants to alleviate this harm, so every winter, we will announce prevention and first aid methods to the public through leaflets or newspapers, so that they can know what to avoid. We have done this for many years, but recently, reading the newspapers, we still often see tragic incidents of coal gas poisoning. This shows that citizens usually do not pay attention to hygiene. Once poisoned, it is too late to regret. Now, we will announce the avoidance methods to the public again, hoping that everyone will pay attention and not ignore them because they are simple. This is very important. (1) Cause of Poisoning: Coal balls or coal blocks emit a gas called carbon monoxide when they are not burned to a very bright state. This gas is colorless and odorless, and it is often difficult to detect. If you smell it for too long, your breathing will become tight, your face will turn red, you will become dizzy, and your mind will become unclear, as if you are drunk. If the poisoning is too deep, you will die. Even if it is mild, you will be sick for a few days. (2) Prevention Methods: When burning coal or charcoal in a room, be sure to install a chimney or vent pipe. If there is no chimney or vent pipe, you must burn it in a well-ventilated area outside the house until it is very bright before moving it indoors. You should also do this when adding coal. Also, when burning coal indoors, you must open one or two windows to allow air to circulate between the indoor and outdoor air. It is best not to burn coal or charcoal when sleeping at night. If you still burn it, you must not close the doors and windows tightly so that they are not ventilated. In short, when burning anything in a room, you must ensure that the outdoor air and the indoor air can circulate and exchange fully. People in the room should also often go outdoors to relax. (3) First Aid for Poisoning: If someone is unfortunately poisoned by coal gas, quickly move them to a well-ventilated area. Loosen their clothing and perform artificial respiration. The method is as follows: Loosen the poisoned person's clothing, lay them flat, and raise their back with pillows or other objects to allow their lungs to expand. Stand behind their head, slowly lift the poisoned person's arms forward, stretch them over their head, and then slowly lower them to the sides of their body, gently pressing down. Repeat this process until the poisoned person wakes up. After waking up, you should still seek medical treatment to recover your health. Otherwise, there may be underlying health problems, so be careful. It is best to perform first aid and seek Western medical treatment immediately. Although the above is very common, it is very important. Coal companies and coal ball companies in the city should print the above methods into leaflets and distribute them to customers when selling them so that users can be alarmed and pay attention. Although it may be a little troublesome for the sellers, the public will benefit a lot. This is not only related to personal morality but also the responsibility that should be fulfilled in human mutual assistance. I hope everyone will implement it properly."

Dan Yaonan and Others Committed Four Robberies and One Kidnapping 150

▲ Chen Jingwu and Seven Others Released

▲ Escorting Bandits to Detention for a Later Hearing

Fan Defu, the Chinese detective chief, and detectives Jin Yangwu, Liu Ronggen, Zhou Guisheng, and Bao Zhengting, from the Jing'an Temple Police Station, previously arrested 24 male and female kidnappers, including Dan Yaonan, at No. 50 Taopeng Lane, Taopeng Road, and other places, and sent them to the First Special District Court for interrogation and detention. This has already been reported in this newspaper. The Chinese and Western detectives have now discovered that the defendants committed four robberies and helped with one kidnapping. The details are as follows: (1) At around 12:00 AM on July 2 of this year, more than 20 bandits armed with guns broke into the home of Cai Zhaotang, a resident of Ping'an Township, Jiangjing County, Jiangbei, and robbed him of more than 40 silver dollars. They also kidnapped Cai's younger brother, Zhaoting, his aunt, a certain Ms. Cai, and his daughter, Lian'di, 18 years old, his son, Lianbao, 12 years old, and his son, Lianfu (also known as Guan Hou), 10 years old, and fled to the Haimen area. They sent a letter to Cai Zhaotang demanding a ransom of 60,000 foreign dollars. Later, because the Haimen area was encountering government troops suppressing bandits, Cai Zhaoting, Cai Lian'di, and his aunt took the opportunity to escape. Lianbao was taken to Changshu and abandoned on the road. He was found by the police, who took him to the police station. After questioning him, they learned the details and notified Cai's family. On November 23, his mother went to pick him up. Lianfu, a child, was taken to Shanghai, hidden in various places. On the 2nd of this month, after the defendants were arrested, their accomplices knew that the situation was urgent and difficult to hide. On the morning of the 7th of this month, at 2:00 AM, they abandoned Cai Lianfu at the intersection of Dengtuo Road and Broadway Road. Xie Futang, the Chinese detective chief of the General Inspectorate, saw the child crying on the road and took him to the police station. After questioning him, he learned that he was a hostage and sent him to the Jing'an Temple Police Station for temporary custody. (2) Robbery of a steelyard worth five corners from the Zhoujiazui Road No. 2572 sauce garden. (3) Robbery of 57 silver dollars from the No. 3 Jingzhou Road sauce garden. (4) Robbery of 71 dollars worth of property from the Song Renxiang family at No. 453 Kunming Road. Robbery of 400 dollars worth of property from the Mao Guanqing family at No. 897 Waimai Gen Road. Yesterday morning, the case was scheduled to open. The police, along with the victims, sent the 24 male and female individuals, including Dan Yaonan, to the Second Criminal Court of the Special Court. Wang Yaotang, the police lawyer, stated the previous situation, saying that Chen Jingwu, Wu Zengcai, Li Zhizhong, Zhu Chenzhi, Yi Hongfang, Xue Lianghou, and Liu Xueshi, seven people, were not related to the cases, and requested that they be released first. There was also one person, Zhao Songshu. Although there was no evidence against him, he was going to Taopeng Road to find the defendant Zhao Zhenghua when he was arrested, and Zhao had committed several robberies in the concession and had a secret conversation with the defendant Wang Guidi in the prison car. It was found that Wang was related to the Jiangjing kidnapping case, and the police had obtained an official document from the court notifying the Jiangjing County government. Therefore, Zhao Songshu was suspicious and should be allowed to continue to be detained. After Judge Feng Shide verified the confessions, he ordered that Chen Jingwu and the other seven people be released, and Zhao Songshu be detained. Then, the trial of the robbery case began. After each victim testified to the robbery, because it was past noon, Judge Feng briefly questioned the defendants and ordered Dan Yaonan and the others to be detained separately, pending a later hearing. The child Cai Lianfu was still temporarily held in the police station by detectives because his father had not arrived.

Yuan Lai Hang Asks for Quick Resolution of the Confiscated Potato Flour Case 151

▲ Letter to the Anti-Japanese Association

Yuan Lai Hang sent a letter to the Anti-Japanese Association the other day, stating, "Dear sirs, our company's confiscated Dutch potato flour was mistakenly resolved by your council to be confiscated. We have prepared documents stating the reasons and requesting reconsideration. We have been honored to have your council decide to resubmit to the review, and your council has twice sent letters asking our company representatives to attend the review committee for statements, and all original documents have also been submitted for verification. The review committee has also sent personnel to various relevant agencies, such as the banks handling remittances, the shipping companies transporting the confiscated goods, and the telegraph bureau Jianghai Customs, for on-site investigation and verification, and it has been found that the evidence is conclusive and the confiscated goods are indeed Dutch goods, which can be found in today's newspaper regarding the review report of this case. Based on this situation, the injustice suffered by our company before can be clarified to the world. Your council members are all outstanding talents in Shanghai, and they will have a fair resolution on this case, so there is no need to nag again. However, our company's potato flour has been confiscated for four months, and the capital is accumulated and the pain is deep. In the meantime, we have been mistakenly resolved to confiscate the application for reconsideration, take photos and publish the newspapers, hire lawyers, and all kinds of expenses are especially not small. If our company's manager did not work diligently day and night and try his best to support it, and at this time when the market is depressed and the capital is extremely tight, I am afraid that our company would have gone bankrupt before the case was clarified. This difficulty should be understood by all council members who understand the business situation. Now the Shanghai market situation is even more lifeless, and the end of the year is approaching. Although our company is still trying its best to support it, it has actually reached the last stage of lingering and cannot be delayed any longer to wait for your council's calm disposal. For this reason, we have stated the following situation. We respectfully ask your council to consider our company's difficult and urgent situation, which is like the disaster victims turning around in the trenches. We hope that the charities will provide assistance as soon as possible and submit this case for resolution and return it as soon as possible in order to come to life and maintain commerce. The council members' merits will be immeasurable."
