Ms. He also donated 1,000 foreign dollars from Sun Zhesheng and He Yaohuan's travel expenses to the Fourth Plenary Session.

Words and Actions of the Japanese Fleet Arriving in Shanghai 153

▲ Imura's Absurd Remarks

▲ U.S. Ships Pay Close Attention

The Japanese naval training squadron Asama and Iwate, carrying 170 naval students, departed from Etajima on November 17, passing through Zhenhai, Korea, taking routes through Dalian, Lushun, Qingdao and Shanghai. After arriving in Shanghai, they were greeted by Rear Admiral Shiozawa, commander of the First Overseas Dispatch Squadron stationed in Shanghai. The situation of Japanese officials and civilians in Shanghai and the Japanese Club giving a public banquet to the officers and students has been reported in yesterday's newspaper. Unexpectedly, after the fleet commander arrived in Shanghai, he issued an absurd declaration, and the follow-up news and investigation are as follows.

▲ Imura's Rebellious Declaration After the fleet arrived in Shanghai, when the Shanghai Japanese expatriates and naval officers feasted the officers and students of the squadron yesterday, Commander-in-Chief Imura Shintaro issued a declaration, generally saying that the fleet departed from Japan, passing through Korea, South Manchuria, Qingdao and other places to Shanghai. The main purpose of this visit is to enable the officers and students of the two ships to understand the situation in Manchuria, Mongolia, and Shandong, because Dalian is the gateway to South Manchuria, Manchuria and Mongolia are the gateway to Korea, and Qingdao is the gateway to Shandong. The three places are important lands of the empire in terms of national defense and economy, and they are necessary for naval officers and students to know. In the future, in economic warfare and national defense warfare, all ships and officers and students of the team must stand on the first line to fight, and it is even more impossible not to let them know, etc. His ambition for aggression and the fallacy of his words are sufficient to prove his premeditation in this declaration.

▲ Visiting Foreign Warships Yesterday, the fleet commander, Imura, accompanied by Rear Admiral Shiozawa, the commander of the First Overseas Dispatch Squadron of the Japanese Navy stationed in Shanghai, visited the commanders and captains of the naval vessels of the United Kingdom, the United States, Italy, and France stationed in Shanghai. In the afternoon, the students of the two ships went ashore to tour, and in the evening, they attended a public banquet of the First Overseas Dispatch Squadron. In addition to the naval officers and students, the two ships Asama and Iwate had a total of 1,439 officers and soldiers.

▲ History of the Two Ships The training ship Iwate, which came to Shanghai this time, has a displacement of 9,796 tons and was built in the 39th year of the Meiji era. During the Russo-Japanese War, it fought in the waters of Lushun and participated in the battle in the waters of Vladivostok and sank a Russian ship in the waters of Ulsan. The Asama has a displacement of 9,737 tons, was built in the 32nd year of the Meiji era. During the Boxer Rebellion, the ship went to Dagu, in the Russo-Japanese War, the ship blockaded the mouth of Lushun harbor, and during the Sino-Japanese War, the ship also participated. The shells that the ship received during the European War are still preserved on the ship.

▲ U.S. Destroyer Follows When the two Japanese ships sailed into Shanghai, the U.S. destroyer No. 226, the Barray, followed the Japanese ships into the Huangpu River. After the Japanese ships docked in Shanghai, the U.S. ships also berthed at the Meifu Wharf. According to Commander Imura yesterday, the ships will leave Shanghai at dawn on the 20th and return to Japan. On March 1 of next year, they will conduct a long-distance cruise, carrying the same group of students to the South Pacific Islands and East Indies, Australia.

After the Great Virtue Wheel Fire, the Chu Heng Wheel Sails to Handle the Aftermath 154

▲ The Great Yu Wheel Sails to Inspect with Passengers and Merchants

▲ The Exact Number of Deaths is Difficult to Determine at This Time

After the Great Virtue Wheel of the Shanghai Dalian Company was destroyed by fire, the company sent the Chu Heng Wheel yesterday to handle the aftermath, and the Great Yu Wheel sailed with passengers and merchants to inspect. The exact number of deaths has not yet been determined. The details are listed below.

▲ Handling the Aftermath The company's board of directors believed that the Chu Yuan Wheel was salvaging corpses at the site of the accident of the Xu Yuan Wheel, but because the river surface was wide, no corpses had been salvaged. Therefore, the Chu Heng Wheel was sent from Shanghai at 0:30 AM yesterday to help the Chu Yuan Wheel salvage corpses and handle the aftermath, and to try to tow back the hull of the Great Virtue Wheel.

▲ Emergency Notice The company issued an emergency notice yesterday, stating that its Great Virtue Wheel set sail on the 12th with 1,052 pieces of cargo and passengers. Unfortunately, on the 13th, when it sailed to the Qiwangsha River surface in Xupu, it suddenly caught fire. It was reported that it was immediately rescued by special vessels. It is now reported that the rescue was ineffective, and the entire ship was destroyed by fire, leaving only the hull. It is currently under investigation whether the cargo is still intact. For fear that various firms will be concerned, in addition to notifying those who know their addresses by special letter, we hereby declare.

▲ Passenger Inspection Passengers and merchants aboard the Great Virtue Wheel are still uncertain whether their cargo was intact after the fire. In order to understand the truth and the situation at the time, they met with various insurance companies and chartered the Great Yu Wheel from the company yesterday. It set sail at 6:00 AM to inspect the site of the accident.

▲ Loading Corpses to Shanghai When the Guangxiang Wheel sailed from Haimen to Shanghai at 2:00 AM yesterday, it loaded the corpse of Luo Jiaham, a teahouse man from the Big Sea Wheel. The company prepared a coffin for burial. At 1:00 PM, when the Daqing Wheel arrived in Shanghai, it loaded the coffin of Xin Lijun, the old rail man from the Great Virtue Wheel, from Yaogang. So far, only 13 corpses of passengers and crew members who died in the disaster have been discovered. Moreover, the exact number of deaths is difficult to determine because those who jumped into the river have drifted away with the waves, and those who were burned to death on the ship cannot be identified.

Establishment of the International Trade Bureau 155

Minister of Industry, Mr. Kong Xiangxi, planned to reorganize the Bureau of Industrial and Commercial Visits into the International Trade Bureau. The details obtained are as follows:

▲Internal Organization The organizational regulations of the International Trade Bureau were first drafted by Mr. Guo and submitted to the ministry for review and transfer. They were revised and passed by the Legislative Yuan and promulgated for implementation by the National Government. The internal structure is divided into four divisions: General Affairs, Guidance, Statistics, and Compilation. Except for the director and deputy director, who are to be appointed by the government, in view of the current national crisis and financial constraints, existing personnel will be redeployed to new positions. ▲Operational Status Although the bureau has been reorganized, the director and deputy director have not yet been appointed by the government. During this transitional period, Mr. Guo, who is preparing the bureau, is temporarily supervising the secretary and the heads of each division to carry out various tasks.

▲Appointment of Advisors According to the provisions of Article 12 of the organizational regulations, experts and those with a well-established reputation in international trade or other economic undertakings may be appointed as honorary advisors. Mr. Guo has specially invited Ma Yinchu, Liu Dajun, Jiang Jingwei, Chen Da, Sheng Jun, He Guang, Zhang Gongquan, Chen Guangfu, Lin Kanghou, Zhou Zuomin, and Tan Danya to be honorary advisors to the bureau.

Lecture on Leprosy Prevention 161

The Women's Support Association of the Chinese Leprosy Relief Association held its regular meeting at the residence of its president, Mrs. Yan Fuqing, yesterday. Dr. Chen Mingkang, director of the Dermatology Department of the Women and Children's Hospital, was specially invited to lecture on the prevention of leprosy. He stated that leprosy was previously thought to be caused by poor food and sin, so lepers were treated cruelly. Later, Dr. Hansen of Norway discovered the leprosy bacillus, and it was learned that leprosy is actually caused by infection. The method of prevention should be to popularize public health knowledge and improve people's living standards. Early treatment should be given to early-stage cases, otherwise, there is a risk of infecting others, and the hope of a cure will be reduced. Therefore, establishing clinics to treat early-stage and non-infectious patients and constructing leprosy hospitals to accommodate severely ill and infectious patients are the most effective methods of dealing with leprosy. If lepers are unwilling to be hospitalized for treatment, and the utensils, clothing, and bedrooms they use are not mixed with others and they adhere to the principle of isolation, the risk of infection can be reduced.

The Municipal Bureau of Public Utilities Urges the Shanghai Telephone Company to Sign a Temporary Contract 164

▲Deadline for Completion is Before the 31st of This Month

▲Otherwise, It Will Be Considered a Voluntary Waiver of Operating Rights

It is found that within the city of Shanghai, the areas outside the Public Concession and the French Concession are all exclusive telephone operating areas of the Shanghai Telephone Bureau of the Ministry of Transportation. In the past, the Shanghai Chinese and Foreign Telephone Company operated telephones in the areas where roads were built across the border in western Shanghai, etc., based on the appendix to the contract signed between the Shanghai Telephone Bureau of the Ministry of Transportation and the Shanghai Chinese and Foreign Telephone Company on December 17th, 14th year of the Republic. The contract term was five years, which expired on December 16th, 19th year. At that time, the Municipal Bureau of Public Utilities was carrying out the automatic telephone conversion project and expanding equipment of the Shanghai Telephone Bureau of the Ministry of Transportation, and there was no supply plan for telephones in the above-mentioned areas. In fact, there was a great need for telephones in this area, and it was difficult to stop the supply. Therefore, it was suggested that the Shanghai Telephone Bureau of the Ministry of Transportation and the Shanghai Telephone Company, which succeeded the Shanghai Chinese and Foreign Telephone Company, negotiate a temporary contract as a transitional measure before a long-term solution was determined. The Shanghai Telephone Bureau of the Ministry of Transportation and the Shanghai Telephone Company both agreed to the proposal, and the Bureau of Public Utilities drafted a temporary contract draft. After meetings and discussions, it was generally agreed. On October 23rd of this year, at the last conversation, the three parties formally signed and acknowledged the draft. Unexpectedly, two months have passed, and the Shanghai Telephone Company has not yet indicated when it can sign the official contract. There is no end to the number of residents in western Shanghai who need to add telephones. Because the contract has not been signed, there is no basis and they can only install and connect slowly. It is now known that the Bureau of Public Utilities has sent a letter to the Shanghai Telephone Company, setting a deadline of December 31st for formally signing the contract, and a written reply must be given before the 25th, so that the official contract can be prepared. If there is no reply after the deadline, the company will be deemed to have voluntarily canceled the temporary contract and waived the operating rights granted by the contract. At the same time, a letter was sent to the Shanghai Telephone Bureau of the Ministry of Transportation, urging the Shanghai Telephone Company to take action. Assuming that the company voluntarily waives these operating rights, the Shanghai Telephone Bureau of the Ministry of Transportation will prepare to supply telephones to the western Shanghai area and complete the work on schedule, so as not to delay the convenience of citizens' telephone calls for a long time.

The Municipal Council Will Ban Obstructions on Roadsides 165

The Municipal Council, in view of the recent obstruction of roads and sidewalks by storefronts, tents, wooden cabinets, advertising boards, and other objects, causing inconvenience to pedestrians, has formulated the following regulations based on Article 23 of the Annex to the Public Concession Land Regulations: (1) Tents or parts thereof shall not be installed lower than seven feet six inches above the sidewalk or fifteen feet above the road surface; (2) No stalls or other movable objects shall be placed in front of any building so as to protrude into the sidewalk or road. These regulations will be implemented from January 1, 1932. Article 23 of the Annex to the Land Regulations originally stated: "Porches, verandas, awnings, push sheds, push windows, steps, cellars, cellar doors, and window awnings made of wood, iron, etc., signboards, window blinds, walls, fences, or any other protruding objects, whether built or placed, that are sufficient to obstruct the safety and passage of the road within the concession, the Municipal Council may notify the resident of the house to order the removal or reconstruction of the obstruction. The resident of the house shall remove or reconstruct the object within fourteen days after receiving the notice, in accordance with the methods indicated by the Municipal Council. If the resident delays in complying, the Municipal Council may impose a fine of not more than ten yuan and remove the obstruction, and the cost shall be borne by the resident and may be recovered according to the example of damages. However, if the obstruction was built or installed by the owner, the cost of removal paid by the resident may be deducted from the rent."

The Municipal Council Builds a New Garbage Incinerator 166

The public concession collects approximately one thousand tons of garbage every day. How to dispose of this garbage is a matter of deep consideration. The methods of disposing of garbage in major cities around the world are roughly three types: (1) stacking in vacant land outside the city, (2) dumping into the sea, and (3) incineration. The public concession has always adopted the first method, but the land for stacking is limited, and the odor cannot be avoided, which is not a long-term solution. If the second method is used, transportation is extremely time-consuming. As for the third method, the cost is the highest, but it is the most hygienic. Recently, the Health Department of the Municipal Council investigated the situation of incinerators used in Europe and the United States. As a result, it was found that the garbage produced in Shanghai contains too few fuel components (such as waste paper and broken wood). Therefore, the existing incineration methods in various places are not applicable. After detailed research, it was decided that the Dur & i type of incinerator from Germany and the Balmer type from the United States could be tried. Therefore, in July and October of last year, contracts were signed with the two companies respectively to build one each. In addition, because the nature of garbage in each district is also different, the Dur & i type furnace was built on Binlang Road by the Suzhou River in the western district, and the Balmer type furnace was built on Maohai Road in the eastern district. These two furnaces are now nearing completion and will be available in the spring of next year. The Dur & i type incinerator has two furnaces, with a total incineration capacity of approximately 240 tons every 24 hours. The Balmer type incinerator has an incineration capacity of approximately 134 tons every 24 hours. The ash remaining after incineration has been completely disinfected and will no longer attract flies. When the two furnaces are opened in the future, a new chapter will be opened in the new construction of Chinese municipalities.

Housing Dispute in Yixin Lane, Nanjing Road 167

The tenants of Yixin Lane on Nanjing Road have been illegally oppressed by the landlord and ordered to move out, resulting in litigation in court. The houses in this location are less than ten years old and are still new. When the tenants first rented, they painfully spent money on decoration, small rent, miscellaneous fees, etc., incurring no small losses, and originally hoped to live and work in peace. Unexpectedly, out of the blue, the landlord suddenly used high-pressure tactics to force them to move. The most painful issue for Shanghai citizens recently is the housing problem, and capitalists often only know their own interests, disregarding the public burden and acting arbitrarily. When this case was first heard, it was a local case, but it suddenly became a primary case. It is now reported that the court hearing will result in a declaration of provisional execution, causing widespread panic. In addition to jointly petitioning the Central Party Headquarters, the National Government, and the relevant departments and bureaus, as well as the municipal party and government agencies, they are also requesting active assistance from various groups.

Two Fashionable Female Corpses 168

Two fashionable female corpses floated to the shore of Gaohang in Pudong yesterday. One was about 22 or 23 years old, and the other was about 17 or 18 years old. Both had short hair and wore high-heeled leather shoes and black coats. Shen Guanlin, the local bailiff, salvaged them and investigated. It was learned that the slightly older one was Ms. Wei, the sister of Sun Zhixin, who lived at No. 3 Lane, Chengyi Lane, Carter Road, Avenue Joffre in the Public Concession and worked as an employee at the Bank of China. The slightly younger one was a teacher at Jiangwan Elementary School. It is said that her parents had betrothed her to someone in her childhood and were now forcing her to marry. She could not abandon her duties at school, so she asked Ms. Sun to act as her agent. It is unknown how she died by drowning. The female teacher may have committed suicide due to arranged marriage, but why did Ms. Sun commit suicide? It is puzzling. The case has been reported to the court for examination.

Robbers Obey Teacher's Orders to Commit Robbery 169

▲Failure to Rob Will Result in Punishment by the Gang Rules

On October 4th, the robber Hu Xingsheng gathered four accomplices, armed with guns, to rob the house of Chen Qing at No. 9 Tongfu Road. They robbed gold, pearl, and diamond jewelry, etc., worth more than 4,000 yuan. Yu Wenjun, who lived in the same house, was also robbed of jewelry and cash, totaling about 600 or 700 yuan. Afterwards, they fled without a trace. After the victim reported the case to the police station, the police received a tip on November 25th that Hu Xingsheng was hiding at No. 285 Caishi Road in the French Concession, so they went to arrest him. Hu confessed that all the ornaments had been sold by Guo Shaoyun, who lived at No. 286 Kai'er Road, so Guo was also arrested. They were taken to the First Court of the Special District and interrogated twice. Because the stolen goods were being retrieved, the hearing was postponed until yesterday. First, the police lawyer Zhang Tianyin presented the case, and then the Chinese detective in charge of the case presented the recovered stolen goods. Then, Hu Xingsheng confessed that he went to rob with four people on that day, driving the victim into a side room and tying them with ropes before going upstairs to search. However, he went to rob this time under the orders of someone else. He had recently become a disciple of someone named A Gan, who ordered him to rob. He was unwilling, but several of his companions said that if he did not obey the teacher's orders, he would be punished by the gang rules, so he did not dare not go. Guo Shaoyun confessed that he was a pawnbroker, and Hu Xingsheng often came to pawn and redeem items, which is how they became acquainted. On October 6th, he brought valuable jewelry to pawn again. Because he thought the price was too low, he suggested that he sell it. Because he had no close friends, he introduced him to a Mr. Xu, who his companions often called "Young Master," so he never suspected that the jewelry had been obtained by robbery. At this point, the victim appeared in court and identified Hu Xingsheng as the robber who pointed a gun at him at the time. The court then ordered the debate to begin. After the debate was over, the judgment was scheduled for the 22nd of this month.

Silent Film "Regaining Light" Premieres in Paris 178

The Paris Grand Theatre is premiering the silent film "Regaining Light," which has never been shown in Shanghai, starting today. The film stars Iisha Lanti, the leading actress in the blockbuster "Spiritual and Carnal Love," and the veteran silver screen actor Las Han Sun. It tells the story of a young woman from a modest family who abandons her elderly father to marry a poor scholar, enduring hardship without complaint. However, once the scholar rises to prominence, he attempts to pursue new pleasures and abandon his old love. Although the outcome does not lead to divorce, it is enough to break the heart of the unfortunate woman. The film depicts the pathologies of evil society and exposes its ills with piercing accuracy, making it a rare masterpiece.

Reader's Letter

Mr. Shi Yucai's Message (International Situation and National Salvation Work) 181

Since the September 18th Incident, our military authorities have been ceding the three northeastern provinces with the word "non-resistance." In terms of diplomacy, not only has there been no progress, but it has gradually turned into failure. Recently, it has been heard that the Yunnan-Guizhou Incident has broken out again, and the national affairs are becoming more dangerous every day. All nationals should rise up to save the country from ruin. Newspapers are the people's mouthpiece, the hub of public opinion, and the compass for the people's actions. Regarding national affairs, they should be responsible for propaganda externally and for criticism and guidance internally. Recently, your newspaper has been calling out for the country in distress, it can be said to be screaming with all its might. With patriotic sincerity, it issues tragic and fervent words, which are truly enough to increase the patriotic heart of the nationals. Yucai respectfully hopes that your newspaper and other newspapers will continue to work hard in order to awaken the compatriots of the whole country to engage in patriotic work to achieve the goal of resisting insults and saving the country. Also, according to what your newspaper published yesterday, Russia will make a serious expression towards Japan. Is this kind of expression superficially tough? The establishment of the Japanese Liaison Cabinet, and Arakawa, who has been living in Russia for a long time, taking office as the Minister of the Army, shows that he attaches great importance to diplomacy with Russia. In the future, he may secretly force Russia to compromise. I think that although the diplomatic relations between China and Russia should not be clearly restored at present, they should be secretly allied with Soviet Russia as soon as possible, and agree to attack Japan together. Moreover, the United States is rich in economic power. Although it often seems calm for the first half of the time, when it moves, its power will be strong. Russia very much hopes for a war between Japan and the United States, and the United States also hopes for a war between Japan and Russia. If Japan and Russia really fight, our country should immediately declare to the world on the surface that China and Russia are acting separately. In this way, China and Russia will be in a de facto cooperation without formal cooperation. Furthermore, Japan and France's secret collusion has gradually been exposed. France is adjacent to Germany and Italy, and was once allied with Russia, and is a long-standing enemy with Britain and Germany. At this time, our country should seem to connect with Germany in order to restrain France. As for Italy, its people are rich in patriotic ideas, so they can stand among the strong countries, but the lack of minerals is indeed a shortcoming of a strong country. However, it is precisely because of this that they are forced to make efforts to develop abroad. I vaguely recall seeing a report a few months ago about the Italian Prime Minister visiting Germany, but I do not remember the details very well. Although the visit is a common etiquette, it actually contains political significance. What is the current international situation after all? According to the current international situation, how will the Second World War proceed? Before the outbreak of the war, our country should work hard on national defense and recover lost territory. When the war starts, our country should take independent action. However, at the appropriate time, our country can also assess the advantages and disadvantages, as well as the strength and weakness of all parties, and formally participate in the war accordingly. Is this an appropriate way? I hope that you will appreciate my eagerness to learn about national affairs and teach me in detail. Also, the National Crisis Conference was produced because of the national crisis and should be realized as soon as possible. It should not delay and waste time, or still follow the official style, fooling people and fooling oneself, then the national affairs will be even more hopeless. I sincerely hope that your newspaper will work hard to call out and awaken the authorities, so that the National Crisis Conference will be realized as soon as possible, and an early determination of the direction to lead the national people to work hard in national salvation. However, before the National Crisis Conference is officially convened, it seems appropriate to issue the following matters to the whole country, (1) Notify all sectors of the country that, given the dangerous environment the country is in, all should put aside their grievances and adopt a spirit of perseverance and decisiveness, and act in unity to save the country. (2) All sectors, agencies, and groups across the country should do their duty. (3) All sectors of the country should practice frugality and, starting from a certain date, stop entertainment for a few days. (4) Designate a certain day for the whole country to be silent for a few minutes, but instruct the national military and police circles to pay attention to local security during this silent period. In this way, the acceleration of the national patriotic work will be influenced and tend towards the actual, and there will inevitably be no small impact on the international community. I pray for your bright teaching.

(Reply) Your letter's speculation on the future changes in the international situation is very accurate. However, based on recent observations, the relationship between Soviet Russia and Japan has not yet reached a serious stage. The future of the East Asian situation is entirely dependent on the economy. The prior and later changes of the British and Japanese monetary systems on the gold standard have significant international impact. In short, with nations standing side by side, any action is entirely based on self-interest as a prerequisite. If it is beneficial to plan, it may not be willing to be the head of the war. Your letter said that China's interest lies in the battle between B and C, and country B's interest lies in the battle between A and C, which is extremely true. The country in the past period was too hopeless. Although we are now through this difficult time, we have only to quickly put politics on track, and at the same time establish a rational and effective economic political symbol, with increasing production and controlling consumption as the only goal. The whole country is of one heart, opening up a path to life from the most dangerous and extremely dangerous. Opportunities are all in front of us, I only fear that we will not use them.

Free Talk

Recollections of a Tortoiseshell Beam 184

— Yan Zi

The county town of Nanhui was built during the Kangxi period of the early Qing Dynasty. Its former site was the Nanhui Guard city. It was built by Qi Jiguang during the Jiajing period of the Ming Dynasty to defend the coast against Japanese pirates. Qi lived in the city, in the house where my friend Xie Rong-sheng now resides. The house is not very large, but its style is very ancient. Fifty years ago, Xie's respected father, Mr. Yanxiang, acquired it from the descendants of Qi at a low price. Yanxiang was good at painting flowers, no less than Bai Yang, and was as famous as Gai Qi Xiang. After moving in, he hired craftsmen to renovate it, and the bright windows and clean tables were completely renewed. When the work was completed, he shared his calligraphy with his closest friends in the art world, enjoying himself. However, whenever there were continuous rainy days, strange noises would come from inside the roof ridge. Xie, who was always stubborn, did not think it was strange. One night, he invited friends to drink in the study, and talking about the past, some advised him to move. Xie casually responded. Amidst the wine and candlelight, the sound came again, exactly like the sound of a kite string. The guests were alarmed. The next day, Xie called a craftsman to dismantle the corner of the house and suddenly discovered an ancient sword. The decoration was ancient and elegant, and the blade was extremely sharp. The handle was inlaid with silver wire and had the small seal characters "Qi Jiguang." Only then did he realize that the sword was making a dragon's roar. The locals heard of it and were fortunate to see it. I don't know if it is still treasured. I should ask Rong-sheng when I have time. The following year, relations between China and Japan deteriorated, and the smoke of war suddenly rose. The land and sea forces were defeated. Could it be that the divine object knew and made an uneasy sound in advance? I record this to show the undiminished power of General Qi.

Bu Chu Ting Cao Zhai Fu's Talk Collection

On the Edge of the Circle of Survival 185

Human society is like a circle. I call this circle the circle of survival. Some people live safely in the center of the circle, called people at the heart of the circle of survival. The rest are crowded on the edge of the circle, called people on the edge of the circle of survival.

What are the people at the heart of the circle of survival? What are the people on the edge of the circle of survival? This can be distinguished by the clothes they wear.

The clothes worn by people at the heart of the circle of survival are not only complete for spring, summer, autumn, and winter, but there are also several sets of clothes for each of the twenty-four solar terms that exactly match the season. Moreover, there are clothes for the morning, clothes for the afternoon, clothes for the evening, raincoats for rainy days, dining clothes for eating, bathrobes for bathing, and pajamas for sleeping. One person's wardrobe can fill a house. In the past, when Kang Youwei spent the winter in Xi'an, Liu Zhenhua asked him what fur coat he wanted and could arrange it. Kang Youwei picked up a pen and wrote down seventy-two pieces of all sizes. Whether he got these seventy-two fur coats is unknown, but this list represents the ambition of someone who wants to be at the heart of the circle of survival.

Last night, a young friend and I passed the entrance of a small pawnshop and saw someone bring a package of clothes to pawn. We went in with him to take a look. The shopkeeper opened the package of clothes, and they were all summer clothes. They were pawned for a total of five yuan. He then took out a pawn ticket, and the shopkeeper calculated that it would cost four and a half yuan. He gave the five-yuan note to the shopkeeper, who found a coat and handed it to him, and gave him fifty cents back. He put the coat on his body and the fifty cents in his pocket. This fifty cents is probably his food expenses for tomorrow?

A moment later, an old woman wearing a lined coat, shivering with cold, brought a cotton-padded coat to pawn, and got one and a half yuan. This old woman and her children at home had not eaten anything for two days. Unable to bear the hunger, she had to pawn her cotton-padded coat to buy rice to feed her children. But although she took care of her hunger tonight, who knows if she will not freeze to death tomorrow?

This old woman and her children are struggling on the edge of the circle of survival, and if they lose their footing, they will fall into the grave! Have those people who live comfortably at the heart of the circle of survival felt the inequality of this world?

Biography of Mr. Zhao of Ningling 186

— Wang Quchang

Zhao of Ningling, whose name is lost. A dwarf with long arms. Had great aspirations. Liked to talk about military affairs. Read the Spring and Autumn Annals and the Zuo Zhuan. Uniquely admired Yang Youji. So he practiced archery. Able to hit people from a hundred paces away. Never missing once. The world was then revering Western firearms. Mr. Zhao viewed them as if they were nothing. Once, he obtained a carved bow from an ancient tomb. The spine had inscriptions, all in worm script. If readable it would say, "Born, same achievement. Dead, same heroism. Three thousand years, resting in the soil. Alas, oh bow." Mr. Zhao treasured it as his life. Never leaving his side. Some spoke of the benefits of firearms. Mr. Zhao looked up and said loudly, "How can they match my bow?" One skilled with firearms arranged a shooting competition. Mr. Zhao hit the target ten times out of ten. The shooter of the firearm did not even reach half. Mr. Zhao was all the more pleased. In the twentieth year of Guangxu, the Japanese affair arose. Mr. Zhao held his bow and generously asked to join the army. The high officials laughed at him for being pedantic. Did not respond. He also spoke of strategies for attack and defense. Also no response. Thereupon, was greatly angered. At that time, Liaoyang had already fallen to the enemy. Mr. Zhao secretly went there. Impregnated arrows with poison. Hid in the thickets every day. Sniped at the enemy. Coming and going fleetingly. Killing hundreds and tens. Ultimately unknown whence the arrows came. Upon hearing of the peace treaty and the cession of Taiwan, Mr. Zhao was all the more angered. He waited for the enemy leader, one Ooyama Iwao. Shot two arrows. Missed. Killed his guards to the left and right. Thereupon, was captured. Starved himself to death. Nearing death, still hoarsely calling, "My bow!"

The Outsider Historian says: In times of national crisis, bravely going to the enemy is only a matter of adapting to righteousness. It is not necessary to calculate the advantages of instruments, the differences of strength and weakness, the count of success and failure. Knowing righteousness, Mr. Zhao's single bow could annihilate a strong enemy. Not knowing righteousness, then millions of soldiers are not enough to guard an inch of soil. Those in the world who compare strength and weakness and calculate success and failure are all petty, forgetful of righteousness, mediocre, and cowardly men. How can petty, forgetful of righteousness, mediocre, and cowardly men plan for the country? But the world only

To Fight for a Survival for Four Hundred Million Compatriots 187

— Written by Song Shouchang

Men plot together. This is why Mr. Zhao died. Alas. Alas. What time is it now? Are there also those who have heard of Mr. Zhao's character and are plotting for themselves?

The Economy of the Northeast and the Interior 188

— Ms. Ye Hua

A few months ago, Japan held a Manchuria-Mongolia Exhibition in Tokyo. The purpose was to encourage its people to invade and seize our Manchuria and Mongolia. On December 12, the Shanghai Education Bureau held an exhibition of patriotic activities of various schools. The aim was to alert the academic community and think about striving to save the country. The meeting lasted for three days. On the last day, Zhang Ke-wei, a member of the Northeast Transportation Committee and a German doctor of economics, was invited to give a lecture on the economic problems of the Northeast and the interior. His words were mostly pertinent. The following is a summary of what he said:

Japan's implementation of the invasion of the Northeast did not start with the September 18th Incident this year, but began with the Russo-Japanese War in 1905. Before the war, the forces in the Northeast all belonged to Russia. After the war, they fell to Japan. From then on, the Japanese Association studied the colonial problem of the Northeast day and night. Operating on the immigration to the Northeast. However, the Japanese people regarded the Northeast as a fearful place. Hesitant to move forward. Even today, due to the direct and indirect relationship with the South Manchurian Railway, the number of Japanese who have moved there is still less than 200,000. It is enough to see that Japan's invasion of China is not for survival, but for the pursuit of wealth and enjoyment. This is evidenced by the statistics of a certain British person. He said that Japan in 1880 and today has indeed seen its population grow day by day. Only the rate of increase in production is several times higher than the increase in population. The Japanese people advertised to the world, claiming to be under pressure to survive and to develop colonies. This is a deceitful statement. This is a self-deceiving statement.

The Japanese people are unwilling to reside in the Northeast, while the people of our country's interior are happy to go to that land. More than a million people go there every year. One after another. This is because natural disasters and man-made disasters are forcing them to do so. The production of these million people can at least support 4 million people. Japan can still survive without the Northeast. China can hardly survive without the Northeast. The seriousness of the Northeast problem is beyond words. Not only that, but our country's international trade has a trade deficit of 400 million taels per year. The exchange of Northeast products with the interior offsets a surplus of 300 million taels. Once the Northeast is no longer ours, then the total peacetime trade deficit will be that our country will lose 700 million taels per year. China today has already felt that the four peoples are unemployed and all the people are haggard. The pain of the future when the people are poor and the wealth is exhausted will be doubled. It is like we can get three bitter meals today. After losing the Northeast, even one and a half meals a day will be difficult to guarantee. Therefore, the Northeast issue is the entire issue of the country. May the people of the country think about it deeply.

Gao Junshan Returns from Europe and the United States to Talk about National Crisis (1) 189

— Ji Ping

Ms. Gao Junshan. In the summer of the year before last, she traveled to the United States again. To continue her studies at Columbia University, her alma mater, for two years. She left the United States this summer. Traveled in Europe to observe the new trends in modern education in various countries. When she first arrived in Geneva, it was when Japan forcibly occupied my Liaoji provinces. It was the most tense moment of the League of Nations. Ms. Gao attended the meeting many times. Personally heard the representatives of various member states express their great theories. And the magnificent spirit of my country's chief representative Shi Chong in negotiating the agreement. Therefore, she has a deeper understanding of the League of Nations' position and the attitude of various countries towards my Northeast problem. She has recently returned to China. It is said that for the sake of the national crisis. Unable to bear the fragmentation of the motherland's mountains and rivers. Eager to take the road. Unable to follow the planned European tour. I regret it very much. Yesterday, I happened to meet the reporter and asked about his feelings on this trip. Cheng happily told me. Rambling talk. Quite insightful. Now summarized into three questions. (1) Should students in our country participate in politics? (2) Dissection of the League of Nations' lack of equality. (3) The reason why our country cannot immediately withdraw from the League of Nations. The following is a special introduction.

Most American students take a very calm attitude towards politics. For example, when reading newspapers. They don't pay much attention. Even if they read the newspaper, it is limited to sports, movies. Science……。 And do not pay attention to political news. Not only elementary and middle school students. College students are also like this. This is in the reading room of Columbia University. A conclusion I have carefully observed. Perhaps people who have served in society and are older. Relatively pay attention to political news. Female students like to watch. That is even less. Because they have little interest in politics. So I don't care much about this issue. It can be said that I don't like to read political news. It is a sign of weak political awareness. They not only do not participate in domestic politics. Also rarely pay attention to international issues. In fact. The speech in the American newspaper. Absolutely free. Discourse. Record. Naturally, it is fully developed. The authority of the newspaper is great. As a rule. Everyone likes to read it. Moreover, American students are not unpatriotic. There is certainly a reason why they don't care about politics. According to my speculation. Perhaps it is because domestic politics is clear. Whether it is domestic affairs or diplomacy. They are all the public servants of the people. 丨丨National civil servants丨丨 are fully responsible. Since the people are very trusting. There is no need to supervise at any time. Or because of geographical relationships. The United States is located between the Atlantic and Pacific Oceans. There is no domestic turmoil. There is no invasion of neighboring countries. The people can live and work in peace. Students can study diligently. So political concepts have also been diluted.

When I arrived in Europe. I also observed it with the same eyes. And the college students in various countries. Obviously different. Newspapers are almost one for everyone. Especially paying attention to political news. I think there are many political changes in various European countries. And the location. Very different from the United States. Strong neighbors are eyeing. Border defense is important. Disputes often occur. This kind of fact. It is easiest to stimulate students' patriotism. So daily necessary reading. Should not be ignored. Maybe that's the reason. If you compare our country's students with American students. That is very different. Almost all students above junior high school in our country pay attention to reading newspapers. Pay attention to the news in politics. The more the country is in trouble. The more you want to read the newspaper. The more corrupt politics are. The more you want to participate in politics. For example, now that the national crisis is urgent. The government's response is wrong. Saving the country and protecting the people. When there is no way. Students can no longer study with peace of mind. You can no longer tend to interfere with one of the political issues.

Going on an Expedition 190

— A member of the Youth Aid-to-Ma Army Corps

(2) Leaving Shanghai

Chairman Jiang told us. Now "good men want to be soldiers." I deeply understood Jiang's instructions. So. I didn't care about anything. And resolutely went on an expedition.

On the morning of the 7th. We marched out of the North Station in the grateful cheers of the Shanghai people. There were many people watching along the way. It's like watching a lantern festival. But. Some women sadly shed tears.

More than a hundred Shanghai volunteers. Sent us all the way to Zhenru Station. When they went back. They said goodbye to us very sincerely. They said. "Dear young comrades. We're going back for now. I hope you stand on the front line and bravely kill the Japanese slaves. Recover the three northeastern provinces. We will follow you soon." When they said this. Their eyes were full of tears. Ten out of ten in our team were also sobbing. My old friend Qian Yingjun. He was the saddest. He actually burst into tears. I advised him. "A real man bleeds but does not weep. Why be as knowledgeable as women." However. Under this tragic situation. It will indeed make people extremely sad.

In Zhenru. We are hosted by the Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association of Dada College. Living in the Science Museum. Meals are also provided by them. It is said that their students donated to various restaurants. I didn't ask them. I don't know for sure.

On the 8th. We spent the whole day doing military training on the Dada playground. Have not moved forward. Because Commander Zhang wanted to go to Shanghai to send a telegram to General Ma. And contact the rear affairs. At the same time, our cadres must also be reorganized. Work is very busy.

Rotary Club Story Collection

Sharing Hatred with the Enemy (15) 191

— Gu Mingdao

Chapter 4: Righteousness Obliterates Kinship

The two escaped from the tiger's mouth. They traveled day and night to T City. By this time, the news of the fall of S City had already spread throughout the city. It was known that the Sun Army had occupied S City. All the mortar factories, aircraft factories, and arsenals were seized. The essence of the Northeast was utterly lost. They aided the enemy with the spoils of war. A great golden city was handed over without a fight. Hua Naiqiang couldn't help but cry out loud. Zhongshu comforted him, saying, "These strong armor and sharp weapons are usually only used for personal gain. They were never meant to defend the borders. Why are you crying about it? If our people can sincerely repent and make a comeback, then flattening the three islands will be nothing. Otherwise, crying is useless." Then Zhongshu led him to see her father, Peng Meiguo, and reported their escape. Meiguo was very happy to see his beloved daughter return safely. He also showed Hua Naiqiang some courtesy. From then on, Hua Naiqiang stayed at Peng Meiguo's residence. However, reports of the Sun Army's military operations kept coming. They occupied the Y trading port. They bombarded Gongzhuling. They burned and looted somewhere. They advanced on somewhere. Aircraft dropped bombs and bombed trains. These many ominous warnings were all transmitted to Hua Naiqiang and Zhongshu. The two of them were almost boiling with rage. The Sun Army didn't have many troops. How could they have such a sweeping momentum in the Northeast in just a few days? Alas, the suffering only added to the misery of the common people. Hua Naiqiang said to Zhongshu, "T City is a vital point on the TA railway. The Sun Army has wolfish ambitions. They want more than they have already gained. I expect they will covet this place soon. I wonder if your father is planning and commanding from his position. If they come, what kind of measures will he take to resist? Or will he not resist?" Zhongshu frowned and said, "Brother Naiqiang, I am ashamed to say that my father is usually incompetent. Moreover, he is old, focused on wealth and status, and addicted to pleasure. He has no courage like Lian Po or ambition like Ma Yuan. Although he has more than 10,000 troops under his command, they are all the troops of Basha and Jimen, lacking combat power. How can they know how to love the country and the people? Recently, my father has gathered several officers every day to discuss in secret. I don't know what methods they have. From what I see, there are no fortifications for defense. How can we resist the Sun Army if they come? When I ask him, he always says that military matters are not for women. He promises to keep you safe. It's really hateful to talk about it." Hua Naiqiang couldn't help but sigh and said, "Then my staying here is also meaningless. In the past, Ban Chao joined the army and went deep into the tiger's den with thirty-six men, beheading the heads of various kings and establishing unparalleled achievements. Now I have only a patriotic fervor. Where can I serve?" At this time, tears welled up in Zhongshu's eyes.

Soaring Financial Gold Prices 192

▲Rumor that the National Government will lift the gold ban

▲Soared more than twenty-eight taels

▲Large buyers actively covering short positions. Yesterday's gold market underwent significant changes again. Flour Market Subjected to Environmental Pressure 202

▲ Buying to Cover Short Positions After Initial Decline

Yesterday, the flour market once again showed signs of sluggishness in the morning. Because the quoted price of foreign wheat fell by about three or four "jiao" (a unit of currency), some people became uneasy. Moreover, due to the upcoming settlement for the current month, many outside speculators wanted to close their positions. Therefore, under the pressure of the environment, the market value for the current month reached a low of 1 tael, 8 qian, 0 fen, and 2.5 li (units of currency). This market value is a new record for the past 35 years. The prices for forward months also generally decreased by about one fen. However, after the market opened in the afternoon, the initial opening was still not good. Subsequently, because short sellers were eager to cover their positions and it was rumored that the standard flour of the Fu and Fu factories had been completely purchased by merchants from other regions, leaving only flour from smaller factories, market sentiment improved and rebounded by more than one fen. As a result, the current month improved by 2.5 li, January decreased by 2.5 li, February decreased by 7.5 li, March and April remained unchanged, and May decreased by 2.5 li.
